<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}

</script><script type="text/javascript">
	var moreId = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftMore").length;
	var less = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftless").length;
	for(i=0; i <= less; i++){
		var lessId = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftless")[i].id;
		var togglebtnId = document.getElementsByClassName("show-btn")[i].id;
		var updateNewVal = document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML;
		var newVallength = updateNewVal.length;
		if(newVallength > 100){
			var text = updateNewVal.substring(0,100);
			document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML = text;
		}else if(newVallength < 100){
			document.getElementById(togglebtnId).classList.add("hide");
		}
		
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}

	var moreId = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftMore").length;
	var less = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftless").length;

		var togglebtnId = document.getElementsByClassName("show-btn")[i].id;
		var updateNewVal = document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML;
		var newVallength = updateNewVal.length;
		if(newVallength > 100){

			document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML = text;
		}else if(newVallength < 100){
			document.getElementById(togglebtnId).classList.add("hide");
		}
		
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}

	var moreId = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftMore").length;
	var less = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftless").length;
	for(i=0; i <= less; i++){
		var lessId = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftless")[i].id;
		var togglebtnId = document.getElementsByClassName("show-btn")[i].id;
		var updateNewVal = document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML;
		var newVallength = updateNewVal.length;
		if(newVallength > 100){
			var text = updateNewVal.substring(0,100);
			document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML = text;
		}else if(newVallength < 100){
			document.getElementById(togglebtnId).classList.add("hide");
		}
		
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}

</script><script type="text/javascript">
	var moreId = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftMore").length;
	var less = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftless").length;
	for(i=0; i <= less; i++){
		var lessId = document.getElementsByClassName("compatibleAircraftless")[i].id;
		var togglebtnId = document.getElementsByClassName("show-btn")[i].id;
		var updateNewVal = document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML;
		var newVallength = updateNewVal.length;
		if(newVallength > 100){
			var text = updateNewVal.substring(0,100);
			document.getElementById(lessId).innerHTML = text;
		}else if(newVallength < 100){
			document.getElementById(togglebtnId).classList.add("hide");
		}
		
	}

<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}

<script type="text/javascript">
var slideIndex = 1;
var objUsed =[];
var objExchange = [];
var objFGI = [];
var objUsedDot =[];
var objExchangeDot = [];
var objFGIDot = [];
var openCount = 0;
var originalUsedObj;
var originalExchangeObj;
var originalFGIObj;
renderPopup();

function plusSlides(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex += n);
}

function currentSlide(n) {
  showSlides(slideIndex = n);
}

function resetGallery(partType) {
	if(openCount == 0) {
		originalUsedObj = objUsed;
		originalExchangeObj = objExchange;
		originalFGIObj = objFGI;
	}
	openCount++
	let partNumber = partType.split("-")[partType.split("-").length-1]
	objUsed = originalUsedObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objExchange = originalExchangeObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	objFGI = originalFGIObj.filter(obj => obj.id.split("-")[obj.id.split("-").length-1] == partNumber);
	slideIndex = 1;

	for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";	
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

}

function renderPopup(){
	let slides = document.getElementsByClassName("mySlides");
  	let dots = document.getElementsByClassName("demo");
  	for(let x=0; x < slides.length; x++){
	  let idslides = slides[x].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = idslides.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = idslides.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = idslides.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsed.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchange.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGI.push(slides[x]);
		  
	  }
	}
  
  	for(let m=0; m< dots.length; m++){
	  let iddots = dots[m].id;
	  var dataobjexchange = iddots.includes('EXCHANGEONLY');
	  var dataobj = iddots.includes('USED');
	  var dataobjFgi = iddots.includes('FGI');
	  if(dataobj == true){
		  objUsedDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjexchange == true){
		  objExchangeDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }else if(dataobjFgi == true){
		  objFGIDot.push(dots[m]);
		  
	  }
  	}
}

function showSlides(n) {
	let i;
   for(let z=0; z< objUsed.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objUsed[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objUsed[z];
			 if (n > objUsed.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objUsed.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsed.length; i++) {
				 objUsed[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objUsedDot.length; i++) {
				 objUsedDot[i].className = objUsedDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objUsed[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objUsedDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objExchange.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objExchange[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objExchange[z];
			 if (n > objExchange.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objExchange.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchange.length; i++) {
				 objExchange[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objExchangeDot.length; i++) {
				 objExchangeDot[i].className = objExchangeDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objExchange[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objExchangeDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }

  
  for(let z=0; z< objFGI.length; z++){
	  let tempSlides;
	  if(objFGI[z].className = "mySlides"){
		  tempSlides = objFGI[z];
			 if (n > objFGI.length) {slideIndex = 1} 
			 if (n < 1) {slideIndex = objFGI.length}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGI.length; i++) {
				 objFGI[i].style.display = "none";
			}
			 for (i = 0; i < objFGIDot.length; i++) {
				 objFGIDot[i].className = objFGIDot[i].className.replace(" active", "");
				  }
			 objFGI[slideIndex-1].style.display = "block";
			 objFGIDot[slideIndex-1].className += " active";
	  }
  }
}
